data-pb-placeholder="Write headline here">U.S. efforts once saved the red wolf. But missteps may push the species back to the brink.</a></div> <div class="blurb normal normal-style " data-pb-field="summary" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">Three decades after they were reintroduced to the wild, there is serious doubt that the species can survive outside zoos.
